        function loadOneTrustScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();

            if (!shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            preloadBannerSdk();

            ONE_TRUST_LIBRARIES.forEach((library) => {
                loadScript(library.url, "text/javascript", library.options);
            });

            if (country === "US") {
                loadCCPAAddon();
            }
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithOneTrustEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithOneTrustEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithOneTrustEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            script.setAttribute("data-domain-script", DATA_DOMAIN_SCRIPT);

            return script;
        }

        function loadCCPAAddon() {
            loadScript(CCPA_ADDON.url, "text/javascript", CCPA_ADDON.options);
        }

        function preloadBannerSdk() {
            const link = document.createElement("link");
            link.href = BANNER_SDK.url;
            link.rel = "preload";
            link.as = "script";

            document.head.appendChild(link);
        }

        function oneTrustLoaded() {
            return !!(window.OneTrust || window.OneTrustStub);
        }

        console.debug('OneTrust setup', countriesWithOneTrustEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !oneTrustLoaded()) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!oneTrustLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (function () {
        function shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            const countriesWithKetchEnabled = {"countries":["IN","HU","SG"]};
            if (!countriesWithKetchEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithKetchEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }
            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithKetchEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }


        function loadKetchScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            if (!shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            window.semaphore = window.semaphore || [];

            window.ketch = function () {
                window.semaphore.push(arguments);
            };

            var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(document.location.search);
            var property = urlParams.has("property") ? urlParams.get("property") : "website_smart_tag";

            var scriptElement = document.createElement("script");
            scriptElement.type = "text/javascript";
            scriptElement.src = "https://global.ketchcdn.com/web/v2/config/fandom/" + property + "/boot.js";
            scriptElement.defer = scriptElement.async = true;

            document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(scriptElement);
        }

        function ketchLoaded() {
            return !!window.ketch;
        }

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !ketchLoaded()) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!ketchLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (async function () {
        // const AIRGAP_URL = '<script
        // data-cfasync="false"
        // src=""
        const AIRGAP_URL = 'https://transcend-cdn.com/cm/54b0c313-5d22-47e5-92fd-f979a37d1ad0/airgap.js';
        const countriesWithAirgapEnabled = [];

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {

            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function loadAirgapScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            const enabled = shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) || airgapScriptForced();

            if (!enabled) {
                return;
            }

            loadScript(AIRGAP_URL, "text/javascript", {
                'data-cfasync': false
            });
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithAirgapEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function airgapScriptForced() {
            return window.location.search.includes('icPreferredCMP=airgap');
        }

        function shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithAirgapEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithAirgapEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            return script;
        }

        console.debug('Airgap setup', countriesWithAirgapEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        let geo = getGeo();

        if (geo === null) {
            geo = await waitForGeo();
        }

        if (geo) {
            loadAirgapScripts(geo);
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
	const useMaxDefaultContentWidth = Boolean(false);

	const defaultContentWidth = useMaxDefaultContentWidth ? 'expanded' : 'collapsed';

	let contentWidthPreference;

	try {
		contentWidthPreference = localStorage.getItem('contentwidth') || defaultContentWidth;
	} catch (e) {
		contentWidthPreference = defaultContentWidth;
	}

	if ( contentWidthPreference === 'expanded' ) {
		document.documentElement.classList.add('is-content-expanded');
	}
</script>

													<script data-name="featured-video-mapped-to-wiki">
	(function () {
		// we can't use mw.config here because it's too early so we need to pass this data in different way
		const videoDetails = {
			mapping: {"mediaId":"sXWp3rZ0","connatixPlaylistId":"36081eca-e784-4e30-87c3-133cf673e447","impressionsPerSession":4},
			impressionsPerSession: 4,
		};
		const videoBridgeCountries = ["AE","AG","AL","AM","AR","AT","AU","AZ","BA","BB","BD","BG","BH","BN","BO","BR","BS","BY","CA","CH","CL","CN","CO","CR","CU","CY","CZ","DE","DK","DO","DZ","EC","EE","EG","ES","FI","FR","GB","GE","GF","GG","GH","GP","GR","GT","GU","GY","HK","HN","HR","HU","ID","IE","IL","IM","IN","IQ","IR","IS","IT","JE","JM","JO","JP","KE","KG","KH","KR","KW","KY","KZ","LA","LB","LK","LT","LU","LV","LY","MA","MD","ME","MK","MM","MN","MO","MQ","MT","MU","MV","MX","MY","NG","NI","NO","NP","NZ","OM","PA","PE","PH","PK","PL","PR","PS","PT","PY","QA","RE","RO","RS","RU","SA","SC","SE","SG","SI","SK","SV","TD","TH","TN","TR","TT","TW","UA","US","UY","UZ","VE","VI","VN","ZA","ZW"];
		const tier3VideoBridgeCountries = ["GB","BE","NL","DE","AU","MX","AR","FR","MD","CA","ES","IT","PE","CO","CL","NZ"];
		let hasVideoOnPage = null;

		function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
			const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
			return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
		}

		function hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki() {
			const impressionsSoFar = Number(getCookieValue('playerImpressionsInWiki')) || 0;
			const allowedImpressions = Number(videoDetails.impressionsPerSession);

			return impressionsSoFar >= allowedImpressions;
		}

		function getCountryCode() {
			try {
				return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo'))).country.toLowerCase();
			} catch {
				return null;
			}
		}

		function isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() {
			const countryCode = getCountryCode();

			if (!countryCode) {
				return false;
			}

			// If it's a default mapping, then check the country whitelist from the default mapping.
			if (videoDetails?.mapping?.isDefaultMapping) {
				// If the wiki is classified as a tier3 wiki, then check the country whitelist from the tier3VideoBridge whitelist.
				const allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis = tier3VideoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedTier3CountryCode) {
					return allowedTier3CountryCode.toLowerCase();
				})

				return allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			} else {
				// If not a default mapping wiki (so it's a wiki mapping), then check the country whitelist from the videoBridge whitelist
				const allowedCountries = videoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedCountryCode) {
					return allowedCountryCode.toLowerCase();
				});

				return allowedCountries.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			}
		}

		window.fandomIsVideoPossible = function () {
			if (hasVideoOnPage === null) {
				hasVideoOnPage =
					videoDetails.mapping &&
					isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() &&
					!hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki();
			}

			return hasVideoOnPage;
		};

		window.canPlayVideo = function () {
			return window.fandomIsVideoPossible()
		};

		if (!window.canPlayVideo()) {
			document.body.classList.add('no-featured-video');
		} else {
			document.body.classList.add('has-featured-video');
		}
	})();
</script>

</p><p><b>Princess Shirahoshi</b>, famous in the world as the <b>Mermaid Princess</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">人魚姫</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Ningyo Hime</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>,<sup id="cite_ref-Mermaid_Princess_4-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Mermaid_Princess-4">[4]</a></sup> is a giant <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sillaginidae" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Sillaginidae">smelt-whiting</a> <a href="/wiki/Merfolk" title="Merfolk">mermaid</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Princess" title="Princess">princess</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Ryugu_Kingdom" title="Ryugu Kingdom">Ryugu Kingdom</a>, as the youngest of <a href="/wiki/Neptune" title="Neptune">King Neptune</a>'s children and the only daughter in the <a href="/wiki/Neptune_Family" title="Neptune Family">Neptune royal family</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Intro_2-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Intro-2">[2]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup>
</p><p>Having been locked up and raised inside an impregnable tower for most of her childhood thanks to the constant threat of <a href="/wiki/Vander_Decken_IX" title="Vander Decken IX">Vander Decken IX</a>, Shirahoshi wishes to know more about the outside world, following the will of her late mother, Queen <a href="/wiki/Otohime" title="Otohime">Otohime</a>. She is also the current incarnation of the <a href="/wiki/Ancient_Weapons" title="Ancient Weapons">Ancient Weapon</a> <a href="/wiki/Poseidon" title="Poseidon">Poseidon</a>, to the knowledge of very few.<sup id="cite_ref-another_name:_Poseidon_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-another_name:_Poseidon-3">[3]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">[9]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-First_Summoning_of_Sea_Kings_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-First_Summoning_of_Sea_Kings-10">[10]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">[11]</a></sup>
</p><p>Shirahoshi was first mentioned by <a href="/wiki/Pappag" title="Pappag">Pappag</a> well before her debut, the starfish claiming he knew her and even promising to introduce the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> to her if they arrived on <a href="/wiki/Fish-Man_Island" title="Fish-Man Island">Fish-Man Island</a> (which would later turn out to be a lie).<sup id="cite_ref-Mermaid_Princess_4-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Mermaid_Princess-4">[4]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Intro_2-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Intro-2">[2]</a></sup>
</p><p>She is a major ally during the <a href="/wiki/Fish-Man_Island_Arc" title="Fish-Man Island Arc">Fish-Man Island Arc</a>.
</p>

			<h3 class="trfc161__header-text">Quick Answers</h3>
		</div>
		<img class="trfc161-logo" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/8941553e-df6a-4310-a080-b9da56fdcbdd" alt="fandom logo">
	</div>
	<div class="trfc161__groups">
			<details class="trfc161__group " data-question-id="31232" data-revision-id="2">
				<summary class="trfc161__question-wrapper">
					<b class="trfc161__question">What is the significance of Shirahoshi's title as the Mermaid Princess in One Piece?</b>
						<img class="trfc161__question-chevron" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/835ea5d8-5dd9-4dc6-83dc-8554b30552d7" alt="toggle section">
				</summary>
				<div class="trfc161__answer">
					<div class="quick-answers__answer-text">
						In One Piece, Shirahoshi is known as the Mermaid Princess. Her title holds significance due to her unique ability to summon Sea Kings, a power she mastered during a battle against the New Fish-Man Pirates. Her title also links to the legend of Poseidon, a figure known for commanding Sea Kings. Additionally, Shirahoshi's absence could cause a national crisis, indicating her vital role in her kingdom.
					</div>
					<div class="trfc161__answer-source">
						Provided by: Fandom
					</div>
					<div class="quick_answers__report-module-root" data-reportable="1"></div>
				</div>
			</details>
			<details class="trfc161__group " data-question-id="31233" data-revision-id="2">
				<summary class="trfc161__question-wrapper">
					<b class="trfc161__question">Why was Shirahoshi raised in an impregnable tower during her childhood?</b>
						<img class="trfc161__question-chevron" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/835ea5d8-5dd9-4dc6-83dc-8554b30552d7" alt="toggle section">
				</summary>
				<div class="trfc161__answer">
					<div class="quick-answers__answer-text">
						The mermaid princess of One Piece, Shirahoshi, was safeguarded in a hard-shell tower during her childhood. This was to shield her from threats like Vander Decken IX. Even the royal guards were limited to a five-minute stay in her room. This stringent protection was due to the risks posed by Vander Decken IX and other potential threats, including a World Noble who attempted to abduct Shirahoshi during the Levely.
					</div>
					<div class="trfc161__answer-source">
						Provided by: Fandom
					</div>
					<div class="quick_answers__report-module-root" data-reportable="1"></div>
				</div>
			</details>
			<details class="trfc161__group " data-question-id="31234" data-revision-id="2">
				<summary class="trfc161__question-wrapper">
					<b class="trfc161__question">What is Shirahoshi's relationship with her mother, the late Queen of Ryugu Kingdom?</b>
						<img class="trfc161__question-chevron" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/835ea5d8-5dd9-4dc6-83dc-8554b30552d7" alt="toggle section">
				</summary>
				<div class="trfc161__answer">
					<div class="quick-answers__answer-text">
						Shirahoshi, the mermaid princess from One Piece, shared a deep bond with her mother, Queen Otohime. As a child, she attended her mother's classes about the surface world. At the age of four, she comforted her tired mother. After Queen Otohime's death, Shirahoshi and her siblings pledged to uphold their mother's legacy and protect each other.
					</div>
					<div class="trfc161__answer-source">
						Provided by: Fandom
					</div>
					<div class="quick_answers__report-module-root" data-reportable="1"></div>
				</div>
			</details>
			<details class="trfc161__group " data-question-id="31235" data-revision-id="2">
				<summary class="trfc161__question-wrapper">
					<b class="trfc161__question">How does Shirahoshi's age and height compare to other characters in One Piece?</b>
						<img class="trfc161__question-chevron" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/835ea5d8-5dd9-4dc6-83dc-8554b30552d7" alt="toggle section">
				</summary>
				<div class="trfc161__answer">
					<div class="quick-answers__answer-text">
						Shirahoshi, the mermaid princess in One Piece, is notably larger than many characters. She can easily conceal Luffy, an average-sized human, with one hand. While Jinbe stands at 301 cm, Shirahoshi's height surpasses this. The specific age of Shirahoshi is not given in the available content.
					</div>
					<div class="trfc161__answer-source">
						Provided by: Fandom
					</div>
					<div class="quick_answers__report-module-root" data-reportable="1"></div>
				</div>
			</details>
			<details class="trfc161__group " data-question-id="31236" data-revision-id="2">
				<summary class="trfc161__question-wrapper">
					<b class="trfc161__question">What is Shirahoshi's role in the Neptune royal family?</b>
						<img class="trfc161__question-chevron" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/835ea5d8-5dd9-4dc6-83dc-8554b30552d7" alt="toggle section">
				</summary>
				<div class="trfc161__answer">
					<div class="quick-answers__answer-text">
						Shirahoshi, the mermaid princess of the Ryugu Kingdom, is the youngest child and only daughter of King Neptune. Raised in a secure tower due to Vander Decken IX's threats, she is also the current incarnation of the Ancient Weapon Poseidon. The Sea Kings acknowledge her as their awaited queen. Her father, Neptune, is prepared to defend her, even at the cost of forsaking Otohime's dream.
					</div>
					<div class="trfc161__answer-source">
						Provided by: Fandom
					</div>
					<div class="quick_answers__report-module-root" data-reportable="1"></div>
				</div>
			</details>
	</div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Appearance">Appearance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D1&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Shirahoshi is a <a href="/wiki/Giants" title="Giants">giant</a>-sized mermaid, approximately the size of her pet <a href="/wiki/Megalo" title="Megalo">Megalo</a> but shorter than her father, and is described as "cute but huge" in her introduction; this makes her roughly eight to ten times the size of Luffy, an average human, excluding the length of her tail;<sup id="cite_ref-appearance_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-appearance-12">[12]</a></sup> she can hold and hide Luffy in one hand alone.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">[13]</a></sup> According to <a href="/wiki/Caribou" title="Caribou">Caribou</a>'s estimation, he put her about seven to eight times the size of a human-sized mermaid.<sup id="cite_ref-Caribou_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Caribou-14">[14]</a></sup> Even as a baby, she was much larger than her mother and brothers, but still small enough to be held in her equally large father's hands.<sup id="cite_ref-Baby_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Baby-15">[15]</a></sup>
</p><p>She has very long, flowing pink hair with an <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Red_bean_paste" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Red bean paste">anko</a>-filled<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">[16]</a></sup> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/taiyaki" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:taiyaki">taiyaki</a><sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">[17]</a></sup> hairgrip. Her breasts are large, even relative to her giant-like size, and much of her upper body is exposed. Her broadly striped tail ends in a ruffle around her waist. She tends to have blush marks on her cheeks due to her shyness.<sup id="cite_ref-appearance_12-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-appearance-12">[12]</a></sup> Shirahoshi has been noted for her beauty, which has been said to rival that of <a href="/wiki/Boa_Hancock" title="Boa Hancock">Boa Hancock</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">[18]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">[19]</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Garp" title="Monkey D. Garp">Garp</a> stated that her appearance alone was beyond everyone's expectations.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">[20]</a></sup>
</p><p>She wears a cleavage-baring yellow <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Halterneck" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Halterneck">halter top</a> covered in pearls with a strap that widens and sticks out on the back of her neck. She also wears clam earrings and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/belly_chain" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:belly chain">belly chains</a> with a cloth hanging down in front. She has a very long light red and pink striped tail.<sup id="cite_ref-appearance_12-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-appearance-12">[12]</a></sup>
</p><p>When she and her family arrived at the <a href="/wiki/Red_Port" title="Red Port">Red Port</a> for the <a href="/wiki/Levely" title="Levely">Levely</a>, she wore a light-blue colored shirt.
</p><p>As a four-year-old, she wore a polka dot <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/crop_top" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:crop top">crop top</a> with straps that floated behind her head and her tail alone was larger than her mother.<sup id="cite_ref-4_years_old_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4_years_old-21">[21]</a></sup> As a six-year-old, she wore a light-colored crop top with floating straps.<sup id="cite_ref-6_years_old_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6_years_old-22">[22]</a></sup>
</p>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Other">Other</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D4&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
