<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality">Personality</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D5&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/39/Shirahoshi_Crying.png/revision/latest?cb=20240814221136" class="image"><img alt="Shirahoshi Crying" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="124" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Shirahoshi Crying.png" data-image-key="Shirahoshi_Crying.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/39/Shirahoshi_Crying.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221136"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/39/Shirahoshi_Crying.png/revision/latest?cb=20240814221136" class="image"><img alt="Shirahoshi Crying" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/39/Shirahoshi_Crying.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221136" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="124" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Shirahoshi Crying.png" data-image-key="Shirahoshi_Crying.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/39/Shirahoshi_Crying.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221136"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Shirahoshi_Crying.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Shirahoshi crying.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Despite her size, Shirahoshi has a very fragile personality. She is easily frightened, and quickly breaks out into crying fits whenever she gets upset, such as the time when <a href="/wiki/Megalo" title="Megalo">Megalo</a> disappeared, when Luffy startled her during their first meeting, and when Luffy says that he does not like her. She is greatly pampered by her family, as she claimed that nobody ever yelled at her before and cried at the fact that Luffy was the first to do so.<sup id="cite_ref-Luffy_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Luffy-23">[23]</a></sup> Whenever someone yells at her, she will interpret this as anger towards her and will start crying, while saying that the offender is scary. In fact, Shirahoshi easily tears up whenever she expresses her emotions such as joy, fear, or sadness.
</p><p>She can be grateful since she willingly hides Luffy from the guards after he saved her from being struck by an axe thrown by Vander Decken IX and also thanks him for rescuing Megalo. She is very considerate of her family and kingdom, saying that leaving Hard-Shell Tower even if she wants to would be a selfish thing for her to do. She is also very polite and addresses everyone with "-sama". She even politely rejected Decken's proposal by saying that "he wasn't her type".<sup id="cite_ref-Decken_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Decken-24">[24]</a></sup>
</p><p>Because of her ten years of solitude, she has very limited knowledge of the world outside her tower, so she is rather curious about it as she asks Luffy about the sun, the animals, and forests, even asking him how he can eat so much despite being so small. She also does not seem to know about Devil Fruits as she called the powers of Vander Decken IX as a curse (although Decken himself also refers to his power as such). Much like the citizens of <a href="/wiki/Kuja" title="Kuja">Kuja</a>, she takes Luffy to be the norm for human males. Also, due to being locked up she has a very low stimulation level, and often becomes overly stimulated due to the events during her time with Luffy, causing her to become emotionally worked up.<sup id="cite_ref-Outside_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Outside-25">[25]</a></sup> Because of her inexperience with proper communication, Shirahoshi accidentally offended some royals who were trying to get her attention.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">[26]</a></sup>
</p><p>She seems to be naive, believing a balloon dummy to be her father and only realizing that it wasn't when she looked at it closer right before being captured (although it was part of their plan to be captured intentionally). Even though she knew Hody was behind her mother's death when Megalo confided her, she did not tell anyone because she wants to honor her mother's last wish of not holding any hatred against the killer, but this ends up being a big mistake since this allows Hody to execute his plans, despite <a href="/wiki/Jinbe" title="Jinbe">Jinbe</a> arguing otherwise.
</p><p>However, regardless of her fragile personality, she is sweet and innocent like a child which is evident when she promised to return to the castle by dinner time after leaving her tower. Shirahoshi is extremely kind as she does not bear any anger or resentment even towards people who have hurt her and her family, as despite Hody killing Otohime and later brutalizing her father and brothers right in front of her, Shirahoshi only tearfully wept. Even though not telling everyone about Hody was a dangerous mistake, this shows that Shirahoshi has a strong and gentle spirit since not hating her mother's killer, even though it was her mother's last wish would be impossible for most people as noted by Jinbe, who is deeply impressed by her resolve and kindness. When Decken nearly destroys Fish-Man Island with <a href="/wiki/Noah" title="Noah">Noah</a>, Shirahoshi shows her bravery for the first time, putting the lives of her people ahead of her own. Even as a World Noble tried to enslave her, Shirahoshi still begged her father not to hate when he prepared to attack the noble.
</p><p>When the Straw Hats left Fish-Man Island, Shirahoshi shows a determination to change, promising Luffy that she will stop being a crybaby.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D6&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Family">Family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D7&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>She has a pet shark named <a href="/wiki/Megalo" title="Megalo">Megalo</a> who was formerly a military pet who served the Neptune Army, whom she loves and doted on very much. Megalo was the only friend she can talk to while being locked up in Hard-Shell Tower. When her beloved shark went missing, Shirahoshi got deeply upset and cried continuously.<sup id="cite_ref-Cry_27-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cry-27">[27]</a></sup> Megalo himself reciprocates Shirahoshi's affections and is extremely protective of her as Megalo was mad at Luffy for making Shirahoshi cry and wasted no time trying to comfort her. Prior to Hody publicly revealing himself as Otohime's assassin, Megalo was the only one who is aware of the truth behind Otohime's death, having secretly confided it in Shirahoshi.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/27/Neptune_Family.png/revision/latest?cb=20240814221139" class="image"><img alt="Neptune Family" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Neptune Family.png" data-image-key="Neptune_Family.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/27/Neptune_Family.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221139"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/27/Neptune_Family.png/revision/latest?cb=20240814221139" class="image"><img alt="Neptune Family" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/27/Neptune_Family.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221139" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Neptune Family.png" data-image-key="Neptune_Family.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/27/Neptune_Family.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221139"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Neptune_Family.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Shirahoshi with her family.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Her father, King <a href="/wiki/Neptune" title="Neptune">Neptune</a>, and her brothers, <a href="/wiki/Fukaboshi" title="Fukaboshi">Fukaboshi</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ryuboshi" title="Ryuboshi">Ryuboshi</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Manboshi" title="Manboshi">Manboshi</a>, all care for her well-being. They gathered an army to hunt down Vander Decken IX, a criminal who kept pestering Shirahoshi with love letters and threatening marriage proposals. King Neptune considers Shirahoshi his treasure. That is the reason they protect her in the hard-shell tower from Vander Decken IX, and the royal guards cannot stay in her room for more than five minutes for the same reason. When a World Noble tried to take Shirahoshi during the Levely, Neptune prepared to fight for his daughter even if it means giving up on Otohime's dream.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">[28]</a></sup>
</p><p>Shirahoshi also greatly missed her deceased mother, <a href="/wiki/Otohime" title="Otohime">Otohime</a>, wanting to visit her grave since it was built. Her love for her mother was so great, the princess went through great turmoil to honor her mother's final wish by not hating Hody for killing Otohime.
</p><p>Her family apparently had been too easy on her since Shirahoshi never had been yelled at until she met Luffy.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Friends">Friends</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D8&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Monkey_D._Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D9&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>At first, Shirahoshi thought that <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a> was an <a href="/wiki/Assassin" title="Assassin">assassin</a> aiming for her life and feared him. However, when he blocked a flying axe that was aimed at her and figured out that he was the one who saved Megalo, she warmed up to him. She even hid him from the guards when they were searching for Luffy after he and his crew were wrongly accused of kidnapping mermaids and after Madam Shyarly's claim of envisioning Luffy destroying Fish-Man Island. When Shirahoshi poked Luffy's face while he was eating, Luffy snapped at her for it. Shirahoshi started crying and tearfully stated that Luffy is the first person to ever yell at her.<sup id="cite_ref-Luffy_23-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Luffy-23">[23]</a></sup> After seeing how fragile Shirahoshi's personality is, Luffy bluntly called her a crybaby and a weakling. However, after getting along with Luffy, Shirahoshi does not show any resentment towards him for calling her names and she was able to leave the tower for the first time in ten years when Luffy offered to protect her. Luffy also stood between her and Vander Decken IX.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/46/Shirahoshi_Crying_Over_Luffy%27s_Departure.png/revision/latest?cb=20240814221145" class="image"><img alt="Shirahoshi Crying Over Luffy's Departure" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Shirahoshi Crying Over Luffy's Departure.png" data-image-key="Shirahoshi_Crying_Over_Luffy%27s_Departure.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/46/Shirahoshi_Crying_Over_Luffy%27s_Departure.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221145"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/46/Shirahoshi_Crying_Over_Luffy%27s_Departure.png/revision/latest?cb=20240814221145" class="image"><img alt="Shirahoshi Crying Over Luffy's Departure" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/46/Shirahoshi_Crying_Over_Luffy%27s_Departure.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221145" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Shirahoshi Crying Over Luffy's Departure.png" data-image-key="Shirahoshi_Crying_Over_Luffy%27s_Departure.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/46/Shirahoshi_Crying_Over_Luffy%27s_Departure.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221145"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Shirahoshi_Crying_Over_Luffy%27s_Departure.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Shirahoshi cries as Luffy is leaving.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Luffy's treatment of Shirahoshi is similar to how <a href="/wiki/Portgas_D._Ace" title="Portgas D. Ace">Ace</a> treated Luffy during their childhood, and how Luffy treated <a href="/wiki/Koby" title="Koby">Koby</a> when they first met: harsh and blunt, but shows some kind of care, and then friendly. She trusts in Luffy's abilities, acting very carefree out in the open while he is around.<sup id="cite_ref-Laugh_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Laugh-29">[29]</a></sup> After learning how Shirahoshi was able to honor her mother's last wish for so many years, Luffy acknowledged that Shirahoshi is not as weak as he had originally thought. He then calls her "Weakhoshi" since he still considers her a crybaby. Shirahoshi also shows deep concern for Luffy such as when Luffy lost a lot of blood from the wound he received from Hody and when Luffy went after Caribou for the stolen treasures. As the Straw Hats leave, Shirahoshi promises that the next time they meet, she will no longer be a crybaby. Luffy also promises that he will take her to a real forest on the surface.
</p><p>Though she was initially afraid of going to the Levely, Shirahoshi decides to go because she does not want Luffy to call her weak again.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Straw_Hat_Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D10&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Shirahoshi has become good friends with all the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hats</a> and appreciates them all for saving her, her family, and the kingdom from the New Fish-Man Pirates. She even wished for them to stay on the island longer so she can get to know them better. As she gave them all a tearful farewell, the Straw Hats (minus <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Zoro</a> and <a href="/wiki/Franky" title="Franky">Franky</a>) promise to take Shirahoshi to the surface someday.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Nami">Nami</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D11&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>Because they share similar backgrounds, Shirahoshi was quick to befriend <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a>. Because she heard <a href="/wiki/Camie" title="Camie">Camie</a> refer to Nami as Nami-chin, Shirahoshi believes that it is actually her real name and calls her Nami-chin-sama instead of just Nami-sama.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Jinbe">Jinbe</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D12&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>Shirahoshi has known <a href="/wiki/Jinbe" title="Jinbe">Jinbe</a> since she was little and always had respect for him. Jinbe has come to greatly admire Shirahoshi's devotion towards her mother, Otohime, for keeping her promise for not hating Otohime's killer, Hody. Jinbe also states that he will protect Shirahoshi and her ideals.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Monkey_D._Garp">Monkey D. Garp</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D13&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/09/Garp_Escorts_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest?cb=20240814221154" class="image"><img alt="Garp Escorts Shirahoshi" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="158" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Garp Escorts Shirahoshi.png" data-image-key="Garp_Escorts_Shirahoshi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/09/Garp_Escorts_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221154"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/09/Garp_Escorts_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest?cb=20240814221154" class="image"><img alt="Garp Escorts Shirahoshi" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/09/Garp_Escorts_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221154" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="158" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Garp Escorts Shirahoshi.png" data-image-key="Garp_Escorts_Shirahoshi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/09/Garp_Escorts_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221154"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Garp_Escorts_Shirahoshi.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Garp escorts Shirahoshi to Mary Geoise.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Vice Admiral <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Garp" title="Monkey D. Garp">Garp</a> was in charge of escorting Shirahoshi and her family to the <a href="/wiki/Levely" title="Levely">Levely</a> and again back to the Ryugu Kingdom.
</p><p>Shirahoshi is on good terms with Garp due to him being Luffy's grandfather, they were friendly with each other, and she felt comfortable asking him questions and waved to him as she left with her family for the Levely.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">[30]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Friends_of_the_Straw_Hats">Friends of the Straw Hats</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D14&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6e/Shirahoshi%2C_Vivi_and_Rebecca_Become_Friends.png/revision/latest?cb=20240615233633" class="image"><img alt="Shirahoshi, Vivi and Rebecca Become Friends" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="122" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Shirahoshi, Vivi and Rebecca Become Friends.png" data-image-key="Shirahoshi%2C_Vivi_and_Rebecca_Become_Friends.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6e/Shirahoshi%2C_Vivi_and_Rebecca_Become_Friends.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240615233633"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6e/Shirahoshi%2C_Vivi_and_Rebecca_Become_Friends.png/revision/latest?cb=20240615233633" class="image"><img alt="Shirahoshi, Vivi and Rebecca Become Friends" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6e/Shirahoshi%2C_Vivi_and_Rebecca_Become_Friends.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240615233633" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="122" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Shirahoshi, Vivi and Rebecca Become Friends.png" data-image-key="Shirahoshi%2C_Vivi_and_Rebecca_Become_Friends.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6e/Shirahoshi%2C_Vivi_and_Rebecca_Become_Friends.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240615233633"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Shirahoshi,_Vivi_and_Rebecca_Become_Friends.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Shirahoshi, Vivi, and Rebecca become friends.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>At <a href="/wiki/Mary_Geoise" title="Mary Geoise">Mary Geoise</a>, Shirahoshi quickly bonded with <a href="/wiki/Nefertari_Vivi" title="Nefertari Vivi">Vivi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Rebecca" title="Rebecca">Rebecca</a> due to having a <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">mutual friend</a> that they are indebted to.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">[31]</a></sup> When <a href="/wiki/Charlos" title="Charlos">Charlos</a> tried to make Shirahoshi his slave, Vivi and Rebecca protested against his actions, and <a href="/wiki/Leo" title="Leo">Leo</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sai" title="Sai">Sai</a> tried to save her. After returning home upon the conclusion of the Levely and learning from <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Garp" title="Monkey D. Garp">Garp</a> about a huge incident concerning Arabasta, Shirahoshi became worried for Vivi's safety.<br style="clear:both;">
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Enemies">Enemies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D15&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Vander_Decken_IX">Vander Decken IX</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D16&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Shirahoshi is terrified of <a href="/wiki/Vander_Decken_IX" title="Vander Decken IX">Vander Decken IX</a> for sending her threatening marriage proposals. Decken is completely obsessed with the Mermaid Princess and will do anything to get her. His obsession has mounted to the point where he plans on killing her if she refuses him, in order to ensure that nobody else could have her except him. Ultimately, she rejects Decken because he was not her type. With her rejection, Decken became hell-bent on killing her. She only survived thanks to Luffy's swift counterattacks.<sup id="cite_ref-Decken_24-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Decken-24">[24]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Hody_Jones">Hody Jones</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D17&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Because of Shirahoshi's ability to summon Sea Kings, <a href="/wiki/Hody_Jones" title="Hody Jones">Hody Jones</a> considers her as a threat to his plans.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">[32]</a></sup> Therefore, she is one of the people that he wants to eliminate the most.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">[33]</a></sup> On the contrary, despite knowing that Hody was the one who murdered her mother, Shirahoshi did not bear a grudge against him nor report his crime to anyone,<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">[34]</a></sup> due to the princess following her mother's final wish of not hating the person who committed the murder. Hody, in return, ridiculed Shirahoshi for her kindness and mercy. <sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">[35]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Charlos">Charlos</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D18&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>When the World Noble <a href="/wiki/Charlos" title="Charlos">Charlos</a> saw Shirahoshi in <a href="/wiki/Mary_Geoise" title="Mary Geoise">Mary Geoise</a>, he made two attempts to make her his slave and would likely have succeeded had it not been for the intervention of Mjosgard and later Sai and Leo.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_2">Other</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D19&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Donquixote_Mjosgard">Donquixote Mjosgard</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D20&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>When Shirahoshi was six years old, a shipwrecked <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Mjosgard" title="Donquixote Mjosgard">Mjosgard</a> threatened her mother with a pistol, which caused great emotional stress that caused the unintentional summoning of a group of <a href="/wiki/Sea_King" title="Sea King">Sea Kings</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">[36]</a></sup> A decade later, Mjosgard rescued her from being enslaved by another World Noble in order to repay his debt to her mother.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">[37]</a></sup> Mjosgard also promised to protect Shirahoshi and her family throughout the Levely.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Abilities_and_Powers">Abilities and Powers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D21&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>As the Mermaid Princess and King Neptune's daughter, Shirahoshi has some level of authority over the kingdom her family rules, however it is unknown how much level of influence she has overall. It was stated by the Minister of the Right that her sudden disappearance from the Ryugu Palace could potentially trigger a nation-wide crisis.
</p><p>Being a gigantic mermaid, Shirahoshi is able to easily lift a normal-sized person with one hand, as she had done with Luffy and Nami. Being a mermaid, Shirahoshi has several abilities unique to her race. It is unknown if she has the ability to talk to regular fish and sea-life like normal mermaids, and call out to them using sonar waves like all the other mermaids and some Fish-Men. Apart from the ability to breathe underwater, as a mermaid she also has the ability to swim very quickly at speeds much faster than other aquatic creatures like the flying fish used by the <a href="/wiki/Flying_Fish_Riders" class="mw-redirect" title="Flying Fish Riders">Flying Fish Riders</a>. As a giant mermaid, she is one of the fastest swimmers in the ocean. However, just like any other mermaid, she is vulnerable on land.
</p><p>Despite her naivete of many things, Shirahoshi has some intelligence. When swimming away from Fishman Island so that Noah would not crush it while chasing her, she realized that since the Straw Hats were the last ones to exit the Ryugu Palace, the gateway between it and the island was still open, allowing her to escape the island's bubble through it.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Poseidon">Poseidon</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D22&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><i>Further information: <a href="/wiki/Poseidon" title="Poseidon">Poseidon</a></i></dd></dl>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/aa/Shirahoshi_Summons_Sea_Kings_as_a_Child.png/revision/latest?cb=20240814221158" class="image"><img alt="Shirahoshi Summons Sea Kings as a Child" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Shirahoshi Summons Sea Kings as a Child.png" data-image-key="Shirahoshi_Summons_Sea_Kings_as_a_Child.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/aa/Shirahoshi_Summons_Sea_Kings_as_a_Child.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221158"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/aa/Shirahoshi_Summons_Sea_Kings_as_a_Child.png/revision/latest?cb=20240814221158" class="image"><img alt="Shirahoshi Summons Sea Kings as a Child" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/aa/Shirahoshi_Summons_Sea_Kings_as_a_Child.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221158" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Shirahoshi Summons Sea Kings as a Child.png" data-image-key="Shirahoshi_Summons_Sea_Kings_as_a_Child.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/aa/Shirahoshi_Summons_Sea_Kings_as_a_Child.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221158"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Shirahoshi_Summons_Sea_Kings_as_a_Child.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Shirahoshi unintentionally summons some Sea Kings.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Shirahoshi has inherited from her ancestor the original Poseidon power with which to command the <a href="/wiki/Sea_King" title="Sea King">Sea Kings</a>. While Merfolk and Fish-Men can summon and communicate with normal fish and marine life via sonar waves, Shirahoshi alone has the uncanny ability to call upon the titanic megafauna of the One Piece world via the same method. By screaming, she emits sonar waves that summons Sea Kings to her. While she was unaware of her power during her childhood, Otohime thought that if she receives a huge shock, she might subconsciously send sea kings on a rampage. However, it is later shown that Sea Kings are intelligent creatures, so this is speculative. Otohime also described this as the most fearsome ability in the world, and that it can change the whole world in great ways. However, in the wrong hands, Shirahoshi's powers can sink the entire world into the ocean. While Luffy was destroying Noah to keep it from crashing into Fish-Man Island, Shirahoshi fully awakened the ability, as she unknowingly summoned the Sea Kings to help save both the ship and the island. Also, when compared to the time she summoned them as a child, Shirahoshi was able to communicate with the Sea Kings perfectly, having briefly spoken to them during the escapade. The Sea Kings then stated that they were called by Shirahoshi's strong desire to help Luffy. It appears that Shirahoshi can summon them through her will and feelings even though she was not directly calling for them. This ability is what classifies her as one of the <a href="/wiki/Ancient_Weapons" title="Ancient Weapons">Ancient Weapons</a> that the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a> fears so much; she is the current incarnation of the weapon <a href="/wiki/Poseidon" title="Poseidon">Poseidon</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-another_name:_Poseidon_3-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-another_name:_Poseidon-3">[3]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Haki">Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D23&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article: <a href="/wiki/Haki" title="Haki">Haki</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p>Like her mother before her, Shirahoshi possesses the ability to use <a href="/wiki/Haki/Observation_Haki" title="Haki/Observation Haki">Observation Haki</a>, though she has yet to demonstrate any use of it.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_7-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-7">[7]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D24&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Past">Past</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D25&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Childhood">Childhood</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D26&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Sixteen years ago, Shirahoshi was merely a baby. But despite this, she was larger than her mother and older brothers. While her mother was away preaching to her people, her brothers would look after her at the palace.<sup id="cite_ref-Baby_15-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Baby-15">[15]</a></sup>
</p><p>When Shirahoshi was four years old, she was seen comforting her exhausted mother and attending her classes when Otohime was teaching about the surface world.<sup id="cite_ref-4_years_old_21-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4_years_old-21">[21]</a></sup>
</p><p>When Shirahoshi was six years old, an uproar had occurred when a <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Mjosgard" title="Donquixote Mjosgard">World Noble</a> arrived at the island in a wrecked ship. Otohime quickly dashed off to where the ship was docked. The four children of the royal family soon followed her to the scene.<sup id="cite_ref-6_years_old_22-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6_years_old-22">[22]</a></sup> When Shirahoshi saw her mother being threatened by the noble she was protecting, she cried and unknowingly called forth <a href="/wiki/Sea_King" title="Sea King">Sea Kings</a>, stunning all those present and making the noble pass out from extreme shock. Shirahoshi, however, was completely oblivious to the Sea Kings.<sup id="cite_ref-First_Summoning_of_Sea_Kings_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-First_Summoning_of_Sea_Kings-10">[10]</a></sup> When Otohime decided to accompany the noble to the surface, Shirahoshi and her brothers looked worried. For one week, she waited in the palace while Neptune tried to cheer her up.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">[38]</a></sup>
</p><p>Otohime returned safe and sound and she held a piece of paper that could make a difference. Shirahoshi and her family were overjoyed that Otohime finally succeeded in getting people's signatures. But that excitement was short-lived.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Threats_of_Hody_Jones_and_Vander_Decken_IX">Threats of Hody Jones and Vander Decken IX</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D27&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/80/Vander_Decken_IX_Marks_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest?cb=20220727165955" class="image"><img alt="Vander Decken IX Marks Shirahoshi" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="263" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Vander Decken IX Marks Shirahoshi.png" data-image-key="Vander_Decken_IX_Marks_Shirahoshi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/80/Vander_Decken_IX_Marks_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220727165955"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/80/Vander_Decken_IX_Marks_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest?cb=20220727165955" class="image"><img alt="Vander Decken IX Marks Shirahoshi" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/80/Vander_Decken_IX_Marks_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220727165955" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="263" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Vander Decken IX Marks Shirahoshi.png" data-image-key="Vander_Decken_IX_Marks_Shirahoshi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/80/Vander_Decken_IX_Marks_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220727165955"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Vander_Decken_IX_Marks_Shirahoshi.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Decken marking Shirahoshi amidst the confusion of her mother's assassination.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>One day in the Gyoncorde Plaza, the box containing all of the signatures caught fire. While the soldiers tried to save the signatures, Otohime was shot. Amidst the chaos, <a href="/wiki/Vander_Decken_IX" title="Vander Decken IX">Vander Decken IX</a> marked Shirahoshi with his <a href="/wiki/Mato_Mato_no_Mi" title="Mato Mato no Mi">Mato Mato no Mi</a> powers. Shirahoshi, who was stunned seeing her mother get shot, did not notice his presence. She was about to scream, but <a href="/wiki/Ryuboshi" title="Ryuboshi">Ryuboshi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Manboshi" title="Manboshi">Manboshi</a> managed to calm her down by dancing and singing in spite of their grief, thus preventing her from summoning Sea Kings subconsciously. As their mother passed away, Shirahoshi and her brothers touched pinky fingers with her for the last time. <a href="/wiki/Megalo" title="Megalo">Megalo</a> was the only one who witnessed Otohime's true murderer and told Shirahoshi. The princess, however, did not tell anyone, in order to fulfill her mother's wish of not hating the culprit.
</p><p>Vander Decken IX, who set his sights on marrying Shirahoshi after witnessing her power, started sending letters to her. Before Otohime's funeral, the four children of the royal family told their father, Neptune, about the love letters that kept flying to Shirahoshi. Neptune told Shirahoshi and her brothers to not go out to the funeral since danger still lurked around. During Otohime's funeral, Shirahoshi and her brothers were seen on a visual broadcast as Fukaboshi gave his speech.
</p><p>Decken kept sending letters to Shirahoshi once a week. Soon, those letters grew into packages. When he started sending threatening marriage proposals, she became so terrified of him that she could not ignore him anymore. Shirahoshi was locked in Hard-Shell Tower for ten years for her safety.<sup id="cite_ref-Tower_39-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Tower-39">[39]</a></sup> For ten years, she wanted to visit the grave of <a href="/wiki/Otohime" title="Otohime">her mother</a> and had many things that she wanted to say to her.<sup id="cite_ref-Otohime_40-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Otohime-40">[40]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Fish-Man_Island_Saga">Fish-Man Island Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D28&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Fish-Man_Island_Arc">Fish-Man Island Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D29&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Her pet shark, Megalo, had been missing for some time, having been captured and held in the Kraken's tentacles. Shirahoshi continued to cry until the shark returned to her, having been freed by Luffy after he defeated the Kraken.
</p><p>When the Straw Hat Pirates were taken to the <a href="/wiki/Ryugu_Palace" title="Ryugu Palace">Ryugu Palace</a>, <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a> wandered off on his own in pursuit of food that smelled good to him. Eventually, he stumbled upon her room, where Princess Shirahoshi was sleeping. <sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">[41]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e1/Luffy_Encounters_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest?cb=20240814221344" class="image"><img alt="Luffy Encounters Shirahoshi" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="121" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Luffy Encounters Shirahoshi.png" data-image-key="Luffy_Encounters_Shirahoshi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e1/Luffy_Encounters_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221344"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e1/Luffy_Encounters_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest?cb=20240814221344" class="image"><img alt="Luffy Encounters Shirahoshi" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e1/Luffy_Encounters_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221344" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="121" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Luffy Encounters Shirahoshi.png" data-image-key="Luffy_Encounters_Shirahoshi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e1/Luffy_Encounters_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221344"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Luffy_Encounters_Shirahoshi.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Shirahoshi finds Luffy in her tower.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Luffy unknowingly walked across her stomach, fell between her breasts, and bounced on them, thinking they were coral due to the coarse material in her top. When she woke up, she became greatly distressed, thinking that Luffy was an assassin targeting her life. She said that she was not scared since she is the daughter of Neptune, but she started crying to no end while calling for help. <sup id="cite_ref-Debut_1-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Debut-1">[1]</a></sup>
</p><p>As she continued crying, an axe thrown by Vander Decken IX came flying into her room aiming for the princess. Luffy deflected the axe, saving Shirahoshi's life. When the guards came to Shirahoshi's room, the princess hid Luffy from them. She told the guards that the noise they heard coming from her room was her having a bad dream. The <a href="/wiki/Minister_of_the_Right" title="Minister of the Right">Minister of the Right</a> explained the situation with the Straw Hats.
</p><p>Once the guards left, Shirahoshi spoke with Luffy. Shirahoshi explained that she had been staying in Hard-Shell Tower for ten years because Vander Decken IX possesses some kind of "<a href="/wiki/Mato_Mato_no_Mi" title="Mato Mato no Mi">curse</a>" which enables him to hit his targets from anywhere. While Luffy was eating, Shirahoshi asked him many questions about the outside world and wondered how Luffy could eat so much while poking him in the cheek. Luffy snapped back and Shirahoshi started to cry, saying that no one had ever yelled at her before. Luffy pointed out that Shirahoshi was a big crybaby, causing her to cry even more. Luffy then offered to take a walk with her outside the castle with him being the bodyguard.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a0/Shirahoshi_and_Luffy_Leave_the_Tower.png/revision/latest?cb=20240814221353" class="image"><img alt="Shirahoshi and Luffy Leave the Tower" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="190" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Shirahoshi and Luffy Leave the Tower.png" data-image-key="Shirahoshi_and_Luffy_Leave_the_Tower.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a0/Shirahoshi_and_Luffy_Leave_the_Tower.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221353"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a0/Shirahoshi_and_Luffy_Leave_the_Tower.png/revision/latest?cb=20240814221353" class="image"><img alt="Shirahoshi and Luffy Leave the Tower" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a0/Shirahoshi_and_Luffy_Leave_the_Tower.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221353" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="190" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Shirahoshi and Luffy Leave the Tower.png" data-image-key="Shirahoshi_and_Luffy_Leave_the_Tower.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a0/Shirahoshi_and_Luffy_Leave_the_Tower.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221353"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Shirahoshi_and_Luffy_Leave_the_Tower.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Shirahoshi leaves inside Megalo.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Luffy asked Shirahoshi about where she wanted to go. The princess said that she wanted to go to the <a href="/wiki/Sea_Forest" title="Sea Forest">Sea Forest</a>. When she started crying again, Luffy started to refer to her as "weakling". Knowing that Shirahoshi's size would draw attention, Luffy came up with a plan. As <a href="/wiki/Brook" title="Brook">Brook</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Minister_of_the_Right" title="Minister of the Right">Minister of the Right</a> arrived at her room, Megalo burst through the doors with Shirahoshi hiding in his mouth.<sup id="cite_ref-Outside_25-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Outside-25">[25]</a></sup>
</p><p>As Shirahoshi, Luffy, and Megalo were leaving, the Mermaid Princess, while thinking to herself, apologized for leaving without permission and promised that she would be back by dinner. Once they left the palace, she then told Luffy how exciting it felt to be outside again, saying it was an adventure. Shirahoshi then told Luffy that in the Sea Forest, there is a grave that she wanted to visit. Shirahoshi and Luffy were then seen laughing together.<sup id="cite_ref-Laugh_29-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Laugh-29">[29]</a></sup>
</p><p>While hovering above Coral Hill, Luffy saw Chopper, Sanji, and a bandaged <a href="/wiki/Hatchan" title="Hatchan">Hatchan</a>. Once Luffy jumped down to meet them, he was met with accusations from the Fish-Man Island citizens for mermaid kidnappings. Megalo had finally reached his limit and spited out Shirahoshi. The Fish-Man Island citizens instantly interpreted this as a Mermaid Princess kidnapping.
</p><p>When Luffy asked her why she got out of Megalo's mouth, she apologized, asking him not to get mad at her. She tried to tell the citizens of Coral Hill that Luffy was only helping her, but they tied him up anyway, along with <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a>, Hatchan, and <a href="/wiki/Tony_Tony_Chopper" title="Tony Tony Chopper">Chopper</a>. She looked frightened when Vander Decken IX showed up. When Decken proposed to her, she rejected him, saying that he was not her type. Enraged, Decken prepared to kill her, and she began to run away, but Luffy told her if she ran away, then he would not be able to protect her.
</p><p>When Decken attacked Shirahoshi, Luffy intercepted his attack while still tied up. She then watched Luffy's fight with Decken which ended with Luffy smashing Decken into the ground. After the fight, Luffy told her to get ready to go, calling her a scaredy cat. Shirahoshi asked him not to yell at her as she was all worked up from the excitement. She then untied Luffy. When the locals asked why she freed him, she apologized to them and promised to be home for dinner. Shirahoshi, Luffy, and his three other friends hopped onto Megalo and headed for the Sea Forest. <sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">[42]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9d/Shirahoshi_Visits_Otohime%27s_Grave.png/revision/latest?cb=20220726232900" class="image"><img alt="Shirahoshi Visits Otohime's Grave" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="136" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Shirahoshi Visits Otohime's Grave.png" data-image-key="Shirahoshi_Visits_Otohime%27s_Grave.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9d/Shirahoshi_Visits_Otohime%27s_Grave.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220726232900"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9d/Shirahoshi_Visits_Otohime%27s_Grave.png/revision/latest?cb=20220726232900" class="image"><img alt="Shirahoshi Visits Otohime's Grave" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9d/Shirahoshi_Visits_Otohime%27s_Grave.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220726232900" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="136" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Shirahoshi Visits Otohime's Grave.png" data-image-key="Shirahoshi_Visits_Otohime%27s_Grave.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9d/Shirahoshi_Visits_Otohime%27s_Grave.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220726232900"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Shirahoshi_Visits_Otohime%27s_Grave.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Shirahoshi visits her mother's tomb.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The group eventually reached the Sea Forest, much to Shirahoshi's delight. They soon met <a href="/wiki/Franky" title="Franky">Franky</a>, <a href="/wiki/Den" title="Den">Den</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Jinbe" title="Jinbe">Jinbe</a>. Luffy introduced the Mermaid Princess to Franky and Jinbe was surprised to see Shirahoshi out of Hard-Shell Tower.
</p><p>After Luffy deflected an axe thrown by Decken, Shirahoshi sat by Queen Otohime's grave and paid her respects.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">[43]</a></sup> Nami and Camie arrived bearing terrible news and Shirahoshi cried when she heard that her father had been captured.
</p><p>Jinbe told Shirahoshi not to worry, saying that he would save her father from the clutches of the New Fish-Man Pirates. Shirahoshi then listened to Jinbe as he explained to the group the back stories of Queen Otohime and <a href="/wiki/Fisher_Tiger" title="Fisher Tiger">Fisher Tiger</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">[44]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d3/Shirahoshi_Befriends_Nami.png/revision/latest?cb=20240814221357" class="image"><img alt="Shirahoshi Befriends Nami" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="158" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Shirahoshi Befriends Nami.png" data-image-key="Shirahoshi_Befriends_Nami.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d3/Shirahoshi_Befriends_Nami.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221357"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d3/Shirahoshi_Befriends_Nami.png/revision/latest?cb=20240814221357" class="image"><img alt="Shirahoshi Befriends Nami" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d3/Shirahoshi_Befriends_Nami.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221357" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="158" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Shirahoshi Befriends Nami.png" data-image-key="Shirahoshi_Befriends_Nami.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d3/Shirahoshi_Befriends_Nami.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221357"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Shirahoshi_Befriends_Nami.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Nami befriends Shirahoshi.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When he finished his account, Shirahoshi began to talk with <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a> and Chopper, brushing back her tears. She explained that she tended to cry whenever she thinks about her mother. She mentioned that she felt strangely comfortable around Nami, who noted that it might be because they have similar backgrounds (both having <a href="/wiki/Bell-m%C3%A8re" title="Bell-mère">lost a mother</a> and were <a href="/wiki/Arlong" title="Arlong">tormented by a Fish-Man</a>).
</p><p>When Hatchan started revealing Hody's plan, a visual <a href="/wiki/Den_Den_Mushi" title="Den Den Mushi">Den Den Mushi</a> appeared and the group watched a visual broadcast by <a href="/wiki/Hody_Jones" title="Hody Jones">Hody Jones</a> himself.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">[45]</a></sup> After Hody explained his plan of creating the new Ryugu Kingdom, which included executing King Neptune, Shirahoshi was about to go back with Megalo, but Jinbe stopped her. Hatchan also told the princess not to go since Hody was using her father as a hostage to safeguard against her ability to summon Sea Kings. After Luffy resolved to fight Hody, Shirahoshi then watched Luffy and Jinbe trying to settle their dispute on how to deal with Hody.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">[46]</a></sup>
</p><p>Shirahoshi was later seen riding on Megalo with Jinbe, heading to Gyoncorde Plaza to save the king. They then saw what barely appeared to be Neptune, floating in the air. As they approached it, it became evident that it was nothing more than a dummy set as a trap, and the three of them got ensnared in a large net. Jinbe, Shirahoshi, and Megalo were then tied up in chains and taken to the plaza. Shirahoshi tearfully apologized to Jinbe for making him fall into such a trap. After Hody revealed to everyone that he was the one who truly killed Otohime, he started gloating about her death right in Shirahoshi's face. The princess, by no means surprised, said that she knew all along.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">[47]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5d/Straw_Hats_and_Allies_Confront_the_New_Fish-Man_Pirates.png/revision/latest?cb=20210222044820" class="image"><img alt="Straw Hats and Allies Confront the New Fish-Man Pirates" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="116" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Straw Hats and Allies Confront the New Fish-Man Pirates.png" data-image-key="Straw_Hats_and_Allies_Confront_the_New_Fish-Man_Pirates.png" data-relevant="1" 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5d/Straw_Hats_and_Allies_Confront_the_New_Fish-Man_Pirates.png/revision/latest?cb=20210222044820" class="image"><img alt="Straw Hats and Allies Confront the New Fish-Man Pirates"
