loading="lazy" width="210" height="116" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Straw Hats and Allies Confront the New Fish-Man Pirates.png" data-image-key="Straw_Hats_and_Allies_Confront_the_New_Fish-Man_Pirates.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5d/Straw_Hats_and_Allies_Confront_the_New_Fish-Man_Pirates.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210222044820"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Straw_Hats_and_Allies_Confront_the_New_Fish-Man_Pirates.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Shirahoshi with Jinbe and the Straw Hats as they confront the New Fish-Man Pirates.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>She knew the truth behind her mother's death because Megalo witnessed the murder at the time and relayed the information to her. However, she concealed the dark secret from everyone because she knew that it would engender more hatred towards Hody, and more importantly she wanted to honor her mother's last wish.
</p><p>Hody laughed and ridiculed her, calling her kindness stupidity. Hody then gloated that because Shirahoshi kept the truth to herself, her father, her brothers, and the citizens of Fish-Man Island were in danger of facing death. When he prepared to kill Neptune, Shirahoshi cried out to Luffy for help, and he jumped out of Megalo's mouth and kicked Hody a great distance away. When the rest of the Straw Hats appeared and lined up, Shirahoshi was seen standing behind them.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">[48]</a></sup>
</p><p>Nami then gave Shirahoshi the World Noble's letter. Luffy commented that Shirahoshi was not as weak as he thought. Jinbe told Shirahoshi that he would help protect her ideals. The princess tearfully thanked everyone for their help. She was then amazed when Luffy defeated half of Hody's forces with <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">[49]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f5/Shirahoshi_Pleads_with_Decken.png/revision/latest?cb=20240814221433" class="image"><img alt="Shirahoshi Pleads with Decken" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="295" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Shirahoshi Pleads with Decken.png" data-image-key="Shirahoshi_Pleads_with_Decken.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f5/Shirahoshi_Pleads_with_Decken.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221433"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f5/Shirahoshi_Pleads_with_Decken.png/revision/latest?cb=20240814221433" class="image"><img alt="Shirahoshi Pleads with Decken" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f5/Shirahoshi_Pleads_with_Decken.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221433" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="295" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Shirahoshi Pleads with Decken.png" data-image-key="Shirahoshi_Pleads_with_Decken.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f5/Shirahoshi_Pleads_with_Decken.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221433"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Shirahoshi_Pleads_with_Decken.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Shirahoshi pleads to Decken to spare her people.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hody and his crew then tried to kill Shirahoshi, but their attempts were thwarted by Jinbe and the Straw Hats. She was then left in the hands of <a href="/wiki/Surume" title="Surume">Surume</a>, who changed sides due to Luffy befriending the kraken.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">[50]</a></sup> However, Hody blackmailed Surume using his brothers and the kraken started squeezing Shirahoshi. Luffy then stepped in by saying he was going to protect Surume's brothers and Surume stopped squeezing.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">[51]</a></sup>
</p><p>Vander Decken IX later arrived at Fish-Man Island while riding on Noah with the intention of crashing the ship into the island. Before the massive ship broke the bubble surrounding Fish-Man Island, Shirahoshi left the plaza and appeared in front of Noah. Shirahoshi offered her own life in exchange for the safety of her people. Vander Decken IX responded by throwing a knife into her shoulder.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">[52]</a></sup>
</p><p>Despite the wound, she fled to the sea to get Noah away from Fish-Man Island. Since the main entrance was too far away, she went through the gateway to Ryugu Palace where she took the straight path into the ocean. Noah followed her without destroying the bubble. Out in the sea, Decken once again demanded that she marry him. Shirahoshi refused and Decken threw knives at her. Ryuboshi and Manboshi blocked the knives in the nick of time. The two brothers then tried to lead Shirahoshi to safety.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/85/Hody_Attacks_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest?cb=20240814221441" class="image"><img alt="Hody Attacks Shirahoshi" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="134" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hody Attacks Shirahoshi.png" data-image-key="Hody_Attacks_Shirahoshi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/85/Hody_Attacks_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221441"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/85/Hody_Attacks_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest?cb=20240814221441" class="image"><img alt="Hody Attacks Shirahoshi" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/85/Hody_Attacks_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221441" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="134" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hody Attacks Shirahoshi.png" data-image-key="Hody_Attacks_Shirahoshi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/85/Hody_Attacks_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221441"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hody_Attacks_Shirahoshi.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hody attempting to kill Shirahoshi.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After Hody dealt a devastating blow to Decken, he attempted to attack Shirahoshi and knocked Ryuboshi and Manboshi away.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">[53]</a></sup> Hody grabbed onto Shirahoshi and prepared to kill her. Shirahoshi was saved when Luffy grabbed Hody and swung him away.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">[54]</a></sup> After learning that the ship would fall on Fish-Man Island if Decken died, Shirahoshi changed her course. Unfortunately, Decken passed out and the ship no longer followed Shirahoshi and began to fall.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">[55]</a></sup> She swam toward Noah, asking Decken to make the ship continue to follow her. Hody tried to attack her using <a href="/wiki/Fish-Man_Karate" title="Fish-Man Karate">Fish-Man Karate</a>, but Manboshi jumped in front of her, taking the attack, much to her disbelief. While Fukaboshi was fighting Hody, she held Luffy's bubble watching the fight.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">[56]</a></sup> Later, after the Ammo Knights arrived, Shirahoshi carried Luffy to Noah while Luffy was talking to Fukaboshi on the baby Den Den Mushi. Hody tried to attack Shirahoshi, but Luffy got between them and intercepted the attack, knocking him away.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">[57]</a></sup>
</p><p>After Luffy defeated Hody onboard Noah, Luffy started destroying the ship. Shirahoshi got scared seeing Luffy's wounds opening up.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">[58]</a></sup> As Luffy continued his barrage, Sea Kings suddenly appeared and held on to Noah, keeping it from falling any further. Luffy, unaware of the Sea Kings, continued his attack until Shirahoshi yelled at him to stop. As Luffy fainted from his open wound, the Sea Kings told Shirahoshi that they were summoned by Shirahoshi's feelings.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">[59]</a></sup>
</p><p>The Sea Kings took Noah to the Sea Forest while Shirahoshi carried Luffy to the plaza. She was frantic since Luffy had lost a lot of blood. She wanted to help Luffy, but she does not have the same blood type as him.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/dd/Caribou_Attempts_to_Capture_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest?cb=20230715142637" class="image"><img alt="Caribou Attempts to Capture Shirahoshi" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Caribou Attempts to Capture Shirahoshi.png" data-image-key="Caribou_Attempts_to_Capture_Shirahoshi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/dd/Caribou_Attempts_to_Capture_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230715142637"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/dd/Caribou_Attempts_to_Capture_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest?cb=20230715142637" class="image"><img alt="Caribou Attempts to Capture Shirahoshi" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/dd/Caribou_Attempts_to_Capture_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230715142637" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Caribou Attempts to Capture Shirahoshi.png" data-image-key="Caribou_Attempts_to_Capture_Shirahoshi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/dd/Caribou_Attempts_to_Capture_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230715142637"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Caribou_Attempts_to_Capture_Shirahoshi.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Shirahoshi nearly abducted by Caribou.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Jinbe volunteered to be Luffy's blood donor, and the Straw Hat captain recovered.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">[60]</a></sup> Jinbe and the Straw Hats quickly left the plaza while Shirahoshi followed them. She begged them to stay a little longer when a royal guard caught up with them. Through a Den Den Mushi, Neptune invited the pirates to a banquet.
</p><p>Shirahoshi attended the banquet with her family and new friends and partook in the celebration.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">[61]</a></sup> Since she does not normally drink, the alcohol made her feel dizzy, so she went to her room. <a href="/wiki/Caribou" title="Caribou">Caribou</a> appeared and attempted to kidnap her after finding out that she is the <a href="/wiki/Ancient_Weapons" title="Ancient Weapons">Ancient Weapon</a> <a href="/wiki/Poseidon" title="Poseidon">Poseidon</a>. Luffy, Zoro, and Sanji showed up and caught Caribou in the act. After Luffy dispatched Caribou by sending him flying outside the palace, Shirahoshi hugged him and thanked him for saving her. She was still shaken from the ordeal when the Straw Hats and the Minister of the Right discussed the disappearance of the palace treasure.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">[62]</a></sup>
</p><p>Later, when the Monster Trio returned to the palace, they informed everyone that Luffy declared war against <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a>. Shirahoshi cheered on Luffy for being strong and got yelled at by <a href="/wiki/Usopp" title="Usopp">Usopp</a>. Shirahoshi started crying and commented on how scary Usopp was.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">[63]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fa/Straw_Hat_Crew_Pinky_Swears_with_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest?cb=20240814221517" class="image"><img alt="Straw Hat Crew Pinky Swears with Shirahoshi" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="120" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Straw Hat Crew Pinky Swears with Shirahoshi.png" data-image-key="Straw_Hat_Crew_Pinky_Swears_with_Shirahoshi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fa/Straw_Hat_Crew_Pinky_Swears_with_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221517"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fa/Straw_Hat_Crew_Pinky_Swears_with_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest?cb=20240814221517" class="image"><img alt="Straw Hat Crew Pinky Swears with Shirahoshi" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fa/Straw_Hat_Crew_Pinky_Swears_with_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221517" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="120" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Straw Hat Crew Pinky Swears with Shirahoshi.png" data-image-key="Straw_Hat_Crew_Pinky_Swears_with_Shirahoshi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fa/Straw_Hat_Crew_Pinky_Swears_with_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221517"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Straw_Hat_Crew_Pinky_Swears_with_Shirahoshi.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Straw Hats making a promise with Shirahoshi.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Later when the Straw Hats were departing Fish-Man Island, Shirahoshi tearfully wished for Luffy to stay longer, which caused Luffy to scold her for crying so much and she apologized. As they left, Shirahoshi swore to Luffy that she would stop being a crybaby. Furthermore, Luffy promised her that if they met again, Luffy would take her to the surface and all the Straw Hats (minus <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Zoro</a> and <a href="/wiki/Franky" title="Franky">Franky</a>) made the same promise as well and Shirahoshi said farewell to all of them.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">[64]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Whole_Cake_Island_Saga">Whole Cake Island Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D30&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zou_Arc">Zou Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D31&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>As the time for <a href="/wiki/Levely" title="Levely">Levely</a> approached, Shirahoshi was asked to accompany her father and brothers. Shirahoshi initially refused, saying that she was too scared and not wanting to break her promise to Luffy. Fukaboshi told her that she should come for their mother's sake.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">[65]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="From_the_Decks_of_the_World:_The_500.2C000.2C000_Man_Arc"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="From_the_Decks_of_the_World:_The_500,000,000_Man_Arc">From the Decks of the World: The 500,000,000 Man Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D32&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Before leaving Fish-Man Island, Shirahoshi and Fukaboshi passed by some children who were wearing "hero hats".<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">[66]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Levely_Arc">Levely Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D33&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>As the Neptune Family prepared to depart Fish-Man Island, Shirahoshi decided to accompany them, not wanting Luffy to call her weak again.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">[67]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4d/Shirahoshi_Sees_Paradise.png/revision/latest?cb=20240814221649" class="image"><img alt="Shirahoshi Sees Paradise" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Shirahoshi Sees Paradise.png" data-image-key="Shirahoshi_Sees_Paradise.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4d/Shirahoshi_Sees_Paradise.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221649"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4d/Shirahoshi_Sees_Paradise.png/revision/latest?cb=20240814221649" class="image"><img alt="Shirahoshi Sees Paradise" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4d/Shirahoshi_Sees_Paradise.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221649" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Shirahoshi Sees Paradise.png" data-image-key="Shirahoshi_Sees_Paradise.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4d/Shirahoshi_Sees_Paradise.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221649"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Shirahoshi_Sees_Paradise.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Shirahoshi sees the surface.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The Neptune Family later arrived at the surface to <a href="/wiki/Red_Port" title="Red Port">Red Port</a>. As <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Garp" title="Monkey D. Garp">Garp</a> escorted them to the bondola, Shirahoshi was showered with attention due to her beauty. The Neptune Family then reached the bondola, and as it ascended to <a href="/wiki/Mary_Geoise" title="Mary Geoise">Mary Geoise</a>, Shirahoshi waved to Garp before gazing and marveling at the sun and the sky.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">[68]</a></sup>
</p><p>Shirahoshi and her family later reached the top of the <a href="/wiki/Red_Line" title="Red Line">Red Line</a> and they made their way to <a href="/wiki/Pangaea_Castle" title="Pangaea Castle">Pangaea Castle</a>. At the socializing plaza, several royals tried to get Shirahoshi's attention, and she was overwhelmed as she accidentally offended them. She then befriended <a href="/wiki/Nefertari_Vivi" title="Nefertari Vivi">Vivi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Rebecca" title="Rebecca">Rebecca</a> after hearing them talk about Luffy.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">[69]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5b/Charlos_captures_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest?cb=20230521192729" class="image"><img alt="Charlos captures Shirahoshi" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Charlos captures Shirahoshi.png" data-image-key="Charlos_captures_Shirahoshi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5b/Charlos_captures_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230521192729"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5b/Charlos_captures_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest?cb=20230521192729" class="image"><img alt="Charlos captures Shirahoshi" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5b/Charlos_captures_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230521192729" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Charlos captures Shirahoshi.png" data-image-key="Charlos_captures_Shirahoshi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5b/Charlos_captures_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230521192729"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Charlos_captures_Shirahoshi.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Charlos attempts to enslave Shirahoshi.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Later, <a href="/wiki/Charlos" title="Charlos">Charlos</a> tried to take Shirahoshi by force. Before Neptune did anything drastic, <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Mjosgard" title="Donquixote Mjosgard">Mjosgard</a> intervened on Shirahoshi's behalf and knocked out Charlos with a spiked club before ordering for Shirahoshi to be set free.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">[70]</a></sup> After Charlos was taken away, <a href="/wiki/Mansherry" title="Mansherry">Mansherry</a> healed Shirahoshi's bruises.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">[71]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Wano_Country_Saga">Wano Country Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D34&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Wano_Country_Arc">Wano Country Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D35&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/47/Charlos_recaptures_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest?cb=20240908021411" class="image"><img alt="Charlos recaptures Shirahoshi" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Charlos recaptures Shirahoshi.png" data-image-key="Charlos_recaptures_Shirahoshi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/47/Charlos_recaptures_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240908021411"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/47/Charlos_recaptures_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest?cb=20240908021411" class="image"><img alt="Charlos recaptures Shirahoshi" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/47/Charlos_recaptures_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240908021411" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Charlos recaptures Shirahoshi.png" data-image-key="Charlos_recaptures_Shirahoshi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/47/Charlos_recaptures_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240908021411"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Charlos_recaptures_Shirahoshi.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Charlos attempts to enslave Shirahoshi again.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>On the fourth day of the Levely, Charlos returned to Pangaea Castle and used <a href="/wiki/Bartholomew_Kuma" title="Bartholomew Kuma">Bartholomew Kuma</a> to recapture Shirahoshi. However, <a href="/wiki/Leo" title="Leo">Leo</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sai" title="Sai">Sai</a> attacked Charlos together, knocking him unconscious, while <a href="/wiki/Morley" title="Morley">Morley</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Revolutionary_Army" title="Revolutionary Army">Revolutionary Army</a> grabbed Kuma and fled.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">[72]</a></sup>
</p><p>After the Levely ended, Shirahoshi thanked Garp for escorting her and the Neptune Family back to Fish-Man Island. When Garp prepared to tell them about a grave incident regarding the <a href="/wiki/Arabasta_Kingdom" title="Arabasta Kingdom">Arabasta Kingdom</a> that occurred shortly after they departed, Shirahoshi began to worry about Vivi.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">[73]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Final_Saga">Final Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D36&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Egghead_Arc">Egghead Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D37&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Back in the Ryugu Kingdom, Shirahoshi and Neptune listened to <a href="/wiki/Vegapunk" title="Vegapunk">Vegapunk</a>'s world-wide message about the world sinking into the sea, Shirahoshi asked her father if it would really happen.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">[74]</a></sup> As the broadcast continued, Vegapunk explained that <a href="/wiki/Joy_Boy" title="Joy Boy">Joy Boy</a> attempted to ensure that the Ancient Weapons would be passed onto future generations, and as one of the Ancient Weapons, Shirahoshi listen in curiosity.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">[75]</a></sup> With the broadcast nearing its end, Shirahoshi listens to Vegapunk continue to talk about the sinking of the world due to the disasters caused by the Ancient Weapons.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">[76]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Translation_and_Dub_Issues">Translation and Dub Issues</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D38&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Shirahoshi's name can be translated as "white star" and may come from <i>Shiro-gisu</i> (シロギス), the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Japanese_whiting" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Japanese whiting">Japanese whiting</a>.
</p><p>When Shirahoshi told Luffy her name, he said it was hard to pronounce. This is probably because of the Japanese linguistic convention <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rendaku" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Rendaku">Rendaku</a>, a vocal phenomenon that tends to morph the pronunciation of certain words when they are used in compound words. For instance, "hoshi" is usually changed to a "B" (boshi), which is what happened with the names of Shirahoshi's brothers.
</p><p>In the <a href="/wiki/Funimation" title="Funimation">Funimation</a> Dub, Luffy referred to Shirahoshi as “Weepyhoshi” instead of “Weakhoshi” after he heard her speech.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Merchandise">Merchandise</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D39&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FShirahoshi%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D43&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d1/Brook_Imagines_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest?cb=20240814221655" class="image"><img alt="Brook Imagines Shirahoshi" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Brook Imagines Shirahoshi.png" data-image-key="Brook_Imagines_Shirahoshi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d1/Brook_Imagines_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221655"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d1/Brook_Imagines_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest?cb=20240814221655" class="image"><img alt="Brook Imagines Shirahoshi" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d1/Brook_Imagines_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221655" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Brook Imagines Shirahoshi.png" data-image-key="Brook_Imagines_Shirahoshi.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d1/Brook_Imagines_Shirahoshi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240814221655"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Brook_Imagines_Shirahoshi.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Brook imagining Shirahoshi.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>After her father mentions the fact that she is big, <a href="/wiki/Brook" title="Brook">Brook</a> (before meeting her personally) imagines her as being big both in size and in width.<sup id="cite_ref-Imagine_77-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Imagine-77">[77]</a></sup></li>
<li>In <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece_15th_Anniversary:_Dive_to_Grand_World" title="One Piece 15th Anniversary: Dive to Grand World">One Piece 15th Anniversary: Dive to Grand World</a></i>, Shirahoshi's height was estimated to be 17 meters.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">[78]</a></sup> However, <i><a href="/wiki/Vivre_Card_-_One_Piece_Visual_Dictionary" title="Vivre Card - One Piece Visual Dictionary">Vivre Card databook</a></i> gives Shirahoshi a specific height of slightly under 12 meters.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_7-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-7">[7]</a></sup></li>
<li>The largest species of smelt-whiting is the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/King_George_whiting" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:King George whiting">King George whiting</a>, growing to a length of 72 cm and 4.8 kg in weight. Overall, the smelt-whitings are a relatively small fish averaging about 20 cm in length and 100g in weight; in contrast to Shirahoshi's size, which is on par with <a href="/wiki/Giants" title="Giants">giants</a>.</li>
<li>Shirahoshi is the second character introduced that <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a> has befriended to whom he has openly stated he "does not like" for being easily scared and cowardly, the first being <a href="/wiki/Koby" title="Koby">Koby</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Chapter_2" title="Chapter 2">second chapter</a>. Coincidentally, both happened at the beginning of their respective "halves" of the story. The first time happened shortly after Luffy began his journey and the second shortly after he resumed it.</li>
<li>Shirahoshi actually shares the same fish species as <a href="/wiki/Mero" title="Mero">Mero</a>, as both are smelt-whiting. They are the only merfolk known to share the same fish species besides the <a href="/wiki/Medaka_Mermaid_Quintuplets" title="Medaka Mermaid Quintuplets">Medaka Mermaid Quintuplets</a>.</li>
<li>In the 5th, 6th, and 7th <a href="/wiki/Popularity_Polls" title="Popularity Polls">fan polls</a> of most popular characters, Shirahoshi was ranked 28th, 32nd, and 50th, respectively, making her the most popular mermaid in the series.</li>
<li>Shirahoshi's birthday, April 4, comes from her name since 4-4 can be derived from Shira-hoshi.<sup id="cite_ref-Birth_6-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Birth-6">[6]</a></sup></li>
<li>Shirahoshi's favorite food is <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Caulerpa_lentillifera" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Caulerpa lentillifera">seaweed grape</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pasta" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Pasta">Pasta</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_7-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-7">[7]</a></sup></li></ul>
